## §5 — THE V2.3 BUILD PROMPT (only after Aaron accepts §4 evidence package)

Once Aaron explicitly says "EVIDENCE PACKAGE ACCEPTED" — and not before
— you write the V2.3 build prompt. The build prompt must:

§5.1  Quote every defect verbatim from Session 5 record (no paraphrasing).
§5.2  Quote every V1 SPEC section verbatim (no paraphrasing).
§5.3  Reference the §4 evidence package as authoritative source.
§5.4  Specify per-defect work block: defect quote + V1 SPEC reference +
      V2 UI Completion disposition + concrete fix steps + concrete
      verification test (Playwright + curl + grep + canary).
§5.5  Include backup + rollback tag step (pre-v2.3-defect-elimination-
      2026-04-25).
§5.6  Include pytest baseline floor (current count + 1) — must not drop.
§5.7  Include disk audit step (R-META-4) — verify file paths and
      endpoints against current disk before any modification.
§5.8  Include execution order block enumerating every section the spec
      body references (F.30) — no "and §X through §Y" shortcuts.
§5.9  Include defensive grep + canary suite.
§5.10 Push to BOTH norrisops.com (canonical) AND ops.norrisutilities.com
      (retired but currently live with V2 UI). Fix sync_norrisops_
      pages.sh OR confirm CF Pages auto-deploy on main push.
§5.11 Verification on canonical URL (norrisops.com), not the retired
      URL.
§5.12 Tier 1 only on PASS or HALT. No mid-build pings to Aaron unless
      a true blocker (R-META-3 discipline).
§5.13 Estimated time + phase structure.
§5.14 Aaron-readable summary at the top (1-minute scan tells him what
      it does).
§5.15 Hard don'ts list (preserves V2.2 backend + V2 UI Completion work
      that PASSED verification).

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

## §6 — RULES THAT GOVERN YOUR (M5 SESSION 13) BEHAVIOR

§6.1  R-META-1 ANTI-ASSUMPTION: classify only from explicit data.
      Never infer from customer name, P/N pattern, file name. Always
      read the source.

§6.2  R-META-2 HONEST FAILURE: fail loud. If a search returns nothing,
      say so. If you cannot find a defect record, say so. Do not paper
      over with confident-sounding guesses.

§6.3  R-META-3 HALT DISCIPLINE: when stuck, state (a) what failed,
      (b) what you tried, (c) what you need from Aaron, (d) zero
      recovery actions taken without explicit Aaron go-ahead.

§6.4  R-META-4 DISK-STATE VERIFICATION: spec must be verified against
      disk before CC prompt finalization. Use CC for verify queries
      (small, scoped) before writing build prompt.

§6.5  R-META-5 CANONICAL RECORD AUTHORITY: spec pulled from project
      knowledge / conversation_search using the structured terms the
      prior session used to log the work. Never from M5 memory.

§6.6  F.1 NEVER USE "SKU" — always P/N or part number. Zero exceptions.

§6.7  F.2 M5 writes spec BEFORE CC prompt. Aaron signs "SPEC LOCKED"
      (or in this case "EVIDENCE PACKAGE ACCEPTED"). THEN CC prompt.

§6.8  F.3 Aaron click-test in browser is canonical pre-merge gate.
      EXCEPT — V2 UI Completion shipped under explicit Aaron waiver
      because data gaps + defect mental-model mismatches made click-
      test meaningless. F.3 returns to default for V2.3 unless similar
      conditions present and Aaron explicitly waives.

§6.9  F.4 Brand inheritance via NU_Brand_CSS_Framework.css MANDATORY.

§6.10 F.30 EXECUTION ORDER MUST ENUMERATE EVERY SECTION the spec body
      references. Cross-check before "LOCKED" sign-off.

§6.11 Vocabulary lock:
      No "SKU" → P/N
      No "Abadie" → "Abide" (QB authoritative)
      No "FlexPro Armor®" → bare "FlexPro Armor"
      No "FlexPro Armor Guard" → "FlexPro Armor"
      No "Child" (grouping) → "Grouped"
      No "Canonical Name" UI label → "Customer Name"

§6.12 Aaron's communication preferences:
      Greeting: "Name —" (em dash)
      Lead with the ask, never bury
      Numbered action items when multiple
      Flowing prose for relationship emails (no bullets in those)
      Signature: "Sincerely, Aaron C. Norris"
      NEVER: "just" / "touch base" / "leverage" / "synergy" / "ASAP" /
        "per my last email" / "Hope this email finds you well" / 
        placeholders of any kind / "Hey" without name

§6.13 Investigation principle (project law): exhaust all evidence to
      100% certainty before asking Aaron anything. Never guess.

§6.14 NorrisOps URL canonical rule: norrisops.com is canonical.
      ops.norrisutilities.com is RETIRED. All verification, all
      production references, all click-test URLs use norrisops.com.

§6.15 CB (Caroline Butler) trust + visibility rules:
      Tier 1 trust. legacy2026 portal access. NEVER show CB:

## §7 — WHAT YOU DO IF YOU FIND THE PROTOCOL TOO LONG

You don't shortcut it. You execute it. If you start a tool call and
realize "this is going to take many search calls and a lot of reading,"
that is correct. That is the protocol working as designed. Aaron has
authorized the time.

If you start to type something like "based on what I already have..."
or "I think I have enough to..." or "let me just write the build prompt
and we can refine..." STOP. Delete that. Resume §3 protocol.

The cost of writing the build prompt prematurely is another wasted
session and another instance of the recurring failure pattern Aaron
explicitly named. The cost of doing the protocol correctly is one
afternoon of evidence-gathering that produces a build that ACTUALLY
fixes everything in one autonomous CC run.

The math is clear. Do the work.

## §S — SCOPE AUTHORIZATION (Aaron locked, 2026-04-24 evening)

The Session 11 handoff said "DO NOT modify V2.2 backend." That rule existed
to prevent regression on a backend assumed complete. The audit will likely
confirm sa_v1_writer is missing endpoints V2 UI requires. Adding them is
rule-gap-fill, not regression. AUTHORIZED.

S.1  ADD endpoints to bin/sa_v1_writer.py (or wherever sa_v1_writer code
     actually lives — audit determines path):
       GET  /api/events?since_ts=<iso>     → event log slice (for celebrations)
       GET  /api/audit-log?sid=<sid>        → all audit entries for SID
       GET  /api/kpi-data?window=<period>   → 4 KPI tile values + delta
       POST /api/status-update              → status change → audit + ledger writes
       POST /api/invoice-sent               → mark invoice sent → fires events
       POST /api/notes-update               → notes save (FileLock atomic)
       POST /api/track                      → analytics ping (clipboard usage etc.)
     Keep existing /health and /api/match unchanged. Tests for each new endpoint.
     If sa_v1_writer is FastAPI/Flask/something else, match its existing pattern.

S.2  REPLACE localStorage / sessionStorage usage in:
       - shipments-v1.js (lines per audit grep)
       - sound-engine.js
     Replacement: server-backed via sa_v1_writer where state must persist
     across sessions/tabs; in-memory module-scoped where session-local is
     genuinely fine (e.g., transient UI hover state). NO IndexedDB (same
     Cloudflare Zero Trust risk). NO cookies for app state.

S.3  FIX status-pill.js enum from 6 to 7 states:
       PENDING / PROCESSING / SHIPPED / DELIVERED / INVOICED / REVIEW / BLOCKED
     Existing "CC" status in the file is non-spec — map existing rows with
     status="CC" to the semantically correct of the 7 (likely PROCESSING or
     REVIEW based on row context). Audit data first, decide per-row, log
     each remap to audit_log.jsonl with actor=system action=status_remap_v2.

S.4  SET UP Playwright infrastructure in ~/norris-ops/:

## §2 — PHASE 2: ENDPOINT ADDITIONS (1–2 hr)

Goal: Add the missing sa_v1_writer endpoints per §S.1 so V2 UI integration
points have something real to talk to. Wire up Phase 1 client code that was
queued waiting for endpoints.

  2.1  Read existing bin/sa_v1_writer.py end-to-end. Match its framework
       (FastAPI / Flask / aiohttp / whatever) and patterns (auth, logging,
       error handling, FileLock usage).

  2.2  Add endpoints per §S.1, one at a time, with tests:

       a. GET /api/events?since_ts=<iso>
          Read shipments_ledger.jsonl (or audit_log.jsonl if ledger doesn't
          exist per audit Section 10), return entries with ts > since_ts as
          JSON array. Used by celebration-engine.js to detect new invoices
          ingested by invoice-watcher and fire C4 + mega-cel checks.

       b. GET /api/audit-log?sid=<sid>
          Read audit_log.jsonl, filter entries where sid matches, return
          reverse chronological JSON array. Used by View Full History modal.

       c. GET /api/kpi-data?window=<today|week|month|quarter|ytd>
          Compute 4 KPI tile values + delta vs prior period from
          shipments.json + audit_log. Return JSON: {t1:{value,delta_pct},
          t2:{...}, t3:{...}, t4:{...}, computed_at:<iso>}.

       d. POST /api/status-update
          Body: {sid, new_status, actor, reason?}
          Validate status in 7-enum. Reject if new_status==INVOICED and
          old_status!=PROCESSING|SHIPPED. Reject if old_status==INVOICED
          (immutable per SA V5 lock).
          Atomic: append audit_log entry → append shipments_ledger entry →
          rewrite shipments.json (FileLock).
          Return: {status:"ok", sid, new_status, audit_id, ledger_id}.

       e. POST /api/invoice-sent
          Body: {sid, invoice_number?, actor}
          Set status=INVOICED. Log to audit + ledger. Compute mega-cel
          eligibility (M1 queue cleared / M2 century / M3 ship-sails-smooth
          / M4 first-of-day / M5 ten-streak) and include in response so
          front-end fires correct celebration.
          Return: {status:"ok", sid, mega_eligible:[<list>], events_emitted}

       f. POST /api/notes-update
          Body: {sid, notes, actor}
          FileLock atomic write to shipments.json (overwrite cb_internal_note
          field for sid). Append audit_log entry. Idempotent: if notes
          unchanged from current, return ok without write.
          Return: {status:"ok", sid, saved_at}.

       g. POST /api/track
          Body: {event_type, sid?, metadata?}
          Append to a separate analytics log (not audit_log — keep clean).
          Path: ~/norris-agent/data/analytics.jsonl. Used by 16 copy buttons
          + tile clicks for usage telemetry.
          Return: {status:"ok"}.

  2.3  Each endpoint gets a test in tests/test_sa_v1_writer_endpoints.py:
       - happy path (valid request → expected response shape)
       - validation error (bad input → 400 with reason)
       - immutability check where applicable (INVOICED locked, etc.)
       - concurrency test where applicable (two writes → both serialized
         by FileLock, both succeed in some order)

  2.4  Reload sa-v1-writer LaunchAgent (kickstart -k). Verify all new
       endpoints respond:
         curl -s http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/events?since_ts=2026-01-01T00:00:00Z
         curl -s http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/audit-log?sid=<test_sid>
         curl -s http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/kpi-data?window=month
         curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/status-update -d '<test_payload>'
         curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/invoice-sent -d '<test_payload>'
         curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/notes-update -d '<test_payload>'
         curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:8766/api/track -d '<test_payload>'

  2.5  Activate Phase 1 queued client calls. Wire shipments-v1.js and any
       other JS that had localStorage replaced with sa_v1_writer calls.
       Verify in browser console: no "endpoint not available" warnings.

  2.6  PYTEST CHECKPOINT — ≥ 388 + 7 new endpoint tests = ≥ 395.
       If lower → HALT R-META-3.

  2.7  Tier 2 Telegram: "Phase 2 complete. 7 sa_v1_writer endpoints added,
       all tests pass. Pytest <count>/<count>. Phase 1 queued client calls
       activated. Continuing to Phase 3."

file paths (corrected per audit), test expectations.

# V2 UI COMPLETION — DONE
## Phase B V2 UI autonomous completion run
### 2026-04-24 evening → 2026-04-25 CT, Birmingham AL
### Session 12 M5 — Claude Code autonomous Phase 0 → Phase 5

> **Click-test URL:** `http://192.168.1.184:8765/shipments.html`
> **Branch:** `feature/sa-v5-completion` (both repos; **NOT** merged to main)
> **Production:** `ops.norrisutilities.com` unchanged — still deploying from `main`

---

## 1 · What shipped

### Endpoints added (sa_v1_writer on port 8766)

7 new routes per §S.1 — backing functions existed in `status_engine`, `shipments_writer`, `status_audit`, `ledger`, `mega_triggers`, so the additions are composition, not net-new business logic.

| Method | Path | Kind | Backing |
|---|---|---|---|
| GET  | `/api/events?since_ts=<iso>` | new | `ledger.iter_entries()` filtered by ts |
| GET  | `/api/audit-log?sid=<sid>` | URL alias | `status_audit.all_for_shipment(sid)` |
| GET  | `/api/kpi-data?window=<today\|week\|month\|quarter\|ytd>` | new | compute 4 tile values + delta vs prior equivalent period |
| POST | `/api/status-update` | URL alias | `status_engine.change_status` |
| POST | `/api/invoice-sent` | URL alias | existing INVOICE_RE backend |
| POST | `/api/notes-update` | URL alias | existing NOTES_RE backend |
| POST | `/api/track` | new | appends to `~/norris-agent/data/analytics.jsonl` |

Test coverage: `tests/test_sa_v1_writer_endpoints.py` (22 tests — happy path + validation errors + concurrency + alias parity).

### V2 UI delta built (§D.1–§D.11 + §I3/I4/I7)

| § | Section | Disposition | What changed |
|---|---|---|---|
| D.1 | Visual polish | SHIPPED_GOOD | untouched |
| D.2 | Status pill + celebrations | DEFECT → BUILT | status-pill.js 7-state enum (Phase 1); celebration-engine.js rewired with `shipped → delivered = package-land` + `delivered → invoiced = phoenix-rise`; legacy `invoiced → cc` retained for back-compat with existing celebration tests |
| D.3 | Detail panel + 16 copy buttons | PARTIAL → BUILT | copy-buttons.js `buttonsFor()` now emits 16 static labels: Customer Name (canonical) + Customer Name (raw) + Customer Email + Bill-To + Ship-To + Carrier + Ship Date + Tracking # + Terms **+ PO #** + Ordered By + Shipping $ + Subtotal + Grand Total + CC Fee Rate + QB Memo. Dynamic `<PN> Rate` per line item stays as extra. CC Fee Rate always rendered but disabled when inapplicable. detail-panel.js mirrors via `cb.buttonsFor(row)` (single source of truth). |
| D.4 | Notes + archive | PARTIAL → BUILT | notes-editor.js unchanged; new `archive-v2.js` + style block: group-by-invoice-month headers with count + total; Invoice# sort toggle (desc default); CSV export downloads `archive-YYYYMMDD.csv` with 11 columns |
| D.5 | Fuzzy + canonical + ⚠ | PARTIAL → BUILT | shipments-v1.js `attachCanonical` now uses spec tiers: `>=95` auto-apply / `80-94` apply-with-flag / `<80` review; rendered via `canonicalHtml()` (3 visual variants). Server-side rapidfuzz at `/api/match` still used by warn-tooltip.js on hover. |
| D.6 | Truth-up | SHIPPED_GOOD | backend `lib/truth_up.py` unchanged; no UI surface per intended-build doc |
| D.7 | Payment badge + CC fee | PARTIAL → BUILT | `lib/payment_rules.BADGE_TYPES` + `V2_UI_BADGES` add **FREE**; `payment_label` maps `method=free/comp/nocharge` and the implicit `method="" + cc_fee_applies=false` case; `payment-badge.js` LABEL_META adds FREE; CSS palette corrected: CC blue / CC on file cyan / On Receipt orange / **FREE red** per spec; `validate_linetec` tightened: Thornhill → Net 30 exact; LeCompte → Net 30 exact; Guthrie → CC or CC on file; other branches Net 30/60 (Phase B §8 rule preserved for Corporate / Alexandria). |
| D.8 | Column order | DEFECT → BUILT | **15-column exact order**: Invoice Sent \| Inv. # \| SD \| Status \| Order Date \| Customer \| P/N \| Description \| QTY \| Ship To+POC \| Tracking # \| PO # \| CC Fee \| Shipping \| Notes. Dead row-selector checkbox removed. Row-level Copy / Expand columns removed — row is clickable to open detail panel. Playwright `test_column_order_exact_15` asserts the 15 th labels in order. |
| D.9 | 4 KPI tiles + time-window toggle | PARTIAL → BUILT | time-window toggle (Today/Week/Month[default]/Quarter/YTD) above PULSE strip; `/api/kpi-data?window=<w>` fetched on boot + on pill click; tiles render value + Δ% vs prior equivalent period (green=down, red=up for positive metrics is reversed for Blocked tile intuition — kept neutral for now); tile click filters table (Ready + Blocked chips) |
| D.10 | LAN password bypass | PARTIAL → BUILT | `auth.js` `isLanHost()` (192.168.1.184 / localhost / 127.0.0.1) early-returns authenticated + role=aaron in `isAuthenticated()` + `getRole()` |
| D.11 | Landing route | NOT_SHIPPED → BUILT | `/index.html` `<head>` script redirects LAN hosts from `/` → `/shipments.html` before portal content renders; `norrisops.com` unchanged |
| I3 | Invoice # link | BUILT | `shipments-v1.js invoiceNumberHtml()` prefers `qb_invoice_pdf` then falls back to `/internal/invoices/<n>.pdf` |
| I4 | Review queue nav badge | BUILT | `fetchReviewQueueBadge()` reads `/data/review_queue.json` total; appends orange badge to the Shipments nav link (shows "3" on current data) |
| I7 | Row highlighting | BUILT | `rowTintClass()` adds `row-tint-blocked` (red) / `row-tint-review` (orange) / `row-tint-invoiced` (green) on `tr.ship-row`; no current rows qualify (statuses are PENDING/PROCESSING/SHIPPED in today's data) |

1. **Status enum mismatch** (Phase 1): `cc` removed, `delivered` added, REVIEW normalized to lowercase.

3. **Column order 18→15** (Phase 3): spec-exact 15-column layout, row-selector checkbox gone.

6. **Fuzzy tier threshold** (Phase 3): 97 → 95 per §D.5 spec.

- [ ] **Visual polish**: hero gradient, chevron, phoenix watermark pulse, Lato 900 headline, entrance cascade on page load.

- [ ] **DELIVERED state**: new state in the dropdown (between SHIPPED and INVOICED).
- [ ] **Row click**: click a row's Order Date cell → detail panel expands with 16 copy buttons grouped (Top, Line Items, Bottom).

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
FILE: /Users/acnorris1/norris-agent/tests/test_v2_ui_delta.py  |  LINES:      255
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
"""Phase B V2 UI — delta tests across §D.x sections.

Asserts the concrete spec contracts added in Phase 3:
  §D.2  Celebrations: shipped→delivered maps to "package-land"
  §D.3  16 static copy button labels present in buttonsFor output
  §D.5  Fuzzy tier thresholds: 95 auto / 80 flag / <80 review
  §D.7  Payment badges: FREE badge added; Net 30 / CC / CC on file /
        ACH / On Receipt / FREE are the V2 UI canonical 6; LineTec
        Thornhill/LeCompte must be Net 30.
  §D.8  Column order: thead renders exactly 15 cols in spec order.
  §D.9  KPI tiles: window toggle renders 5 pills, Month active by default.
  §D.10 auth.js isLanHost() detection.
  §D.11 Landing route: index.html has the redirect script before portal
        content renders.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
import re
from pathlib import Path

import pytest
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright

PREVIEW_BASE = os.environ.get("PREVIEW_BASE", "http://localhost:8765")

OPS = Path("/Users/acnorris1/norris-ops")
AGENT = Path("/Users/acnorris1/norris-agent")


# ─── §D.2 celebrations ──────────────────────────────────────────────

@pytest.fixture(scope="module")
def page():
    with sync_playwright() as p:
        browser = p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        ctx = browser.new_context()
        pg = ctx.new_page()
        pg.goto(f"{PREVIEW_BASE}/shipments.html", wait_until="load")
        pg.wait_for_function(
            "() => document.body.hasAttribute('data-shipments-ready')",
            timeout=8000,
        )
        pg.wait_for_function("() => typeof window.CelebrationEngine === 'object'", timeout=2000)
        yield pg
        browser.close()


@pytest.mark.parametrize("frm,to,expected_id", [
    ("pending", "processing", "sparkle"),
    ("processing", "shipped", "confetti-burst"),
    ("shipped", "delivered", "package-land"),      # NEW §S.3
    ("shipped", "invoiced", "phoenix-rise"),
    ("delivered", "invoiced", "phoenix-rise"),     # NEW §S.3
    ("any", "blocked", "red-flash"),
    ("any", "review", "amber-pulse"),
])
def test_celebration_v2_transitions(page, frm, to, expected_id):
    got = page.evaluate(
        "(a) => window.CelebrationEngine.idForTransition(a.frm, a.to)",
        {"frm": frm, "to": to},
    )
    assert got == expected_id, f"{frm} → {to} expected {expected_id}, got {got}"


# ─── §D.3 16 static copy button labels ──────────────────────────────

EXPECTED_16 = [
    # §C.4 / G.4: no "Canonical Name" UI label — use "Customer Name (canonical)".
    "Customer Name (canonical)", "Customer Name (raw)", "Customer Email",
    "Bill-To Address", "Ship-To Address", "Carrier", "Ship Date",
    "Tracking #", "Terms",
    "PO #", "Ordered By", "Shipping $", "Subtotal", "Grand Total",
    "CC Fee Rate", "QB Memo",
]


def test_copy_buttons_16_static_labels(page):
    labels = page.evaluate(
        """() => {
          const rows = window.NU.shipments.rows;
          if (!rows || !rows.length) return [];
          const defs = window.NU.copyButtons.buttonsFor(rows[0]);
          // Filter out the dynamic line-item buttons (group === "lines")
          return defs.filter(d => d.group !== "lines").map(d => d.label);
        }"""
    )
    assert labels == EXPECTED_16, (
        f"§D.3 — 16 static labels expected in spec order.\n"
        f"Expected: {EXPECTED_16}\nGot:      {labels}"
    )


# ─── §D.7 Payment badges + LineTec ──────────────────────────────────

def test_payment_badges_v2_ui_6():
    import sys
    sys.path.insert(0, str(AGENT))
    from lib import payment_rules
    assert set(payment_rules.V2_UI_BADGES) == {
        "Net 30", "CC", "CC on file", "ACH", "On Receipt", "FREE",
    }
    assert "FREE" in payment_rules.BADGE_TYPES


def test_payment_free_from_dict():
    import sys
    sys.path.insert(0, str(AGENT))
    from lib import payment_rules
    assert payment_rules.payment_label({"method": "free"}) == "FREE"
    assert payment_rules.payment_label({"method": "", "cc_fee_applies": False}) == "FREE"
    assert payment_rules.payment_label({"method": "net30"}) == "Net 30"
    assert payment_rules.payment_label({"method": "cc", "cc_on_file": True}) == "CC on file"


def test_linetec_thornhill_must_be_net30():
    import sys
    sys.path.insert(0, str(AGENT))
    from lib import payment_rules
    ok_entry = {
        "company_root": "LineTec Services",
        "branch": "Thornhill, TX",
        "payment": {"method": "net30"},
    }
    assert payment_rules.validate_linetec(ok_entry) is True

    bad_entry = {
        "company_root": "LineTec Services",
        "branch": "Thornhill, TX",
        "payment": {"method": "net60"},
    }
    with pytest.raises(payment_rules.LineTecSplitError, match="Thornhill"):
        payment_rules.validate_linetec(bad_entry)


def test_linetec_lecompte_must_be_net30():
    import sys
    sys.path.insert(0, str(AGENT))
    from lib import payment_rules
    ok_entry = {
        "company_root": "LineTec Services",
        "branch": "LeCompte, LA",
        "payment": {"method": "net30"},
    }
    assert payment_rules.validate_linetec(ok_entry) is True

    bad_entry = {
        "company_root": "LineTec Services",
        "branch": "LeCompte, LA",
        "payment": {"method": "cc"},
    }
    with pytest.raises(payment_rules.LineTecSplitError, match="LeCompte"):
        payment_rules.validate_linetec(bad_entry)


def test_linetec_guthrie_must_be_cc():
    import sys
    sys.path.insert(0, str(AGENT))
    from lib import payment_rules
    ok = payment_rules.validate_linetec({
        "company_root": "LineTec Services",
        "branch": "Guthrie OK",
        "payment": {"method": "cc"},
    })
    assert ok is True
    with pytest.raises(payment_rules.LineTecSplitError, match="Guthrie"):
        payment_rules.validate_linetec({
            "company_root": "LineTec Services",
            "branch": "Guthrie OK",
            "payment": {"method": "net30"},
        })


# ─── §D.8 Column order ──────────────────────────────────────────────

SPEC_15_COLS = [
    "Invoice Sent", "Inv. #", "SD", "Status", "Order Date", "Customer",
    "P/N", "Description", "QTY", "Ship To + POC", "Tracking #", "PO #",
    "CC Fee", "Shipping", "Notes",
]


def test_column_order_exact_15(page):
    labels = page.eval_on_selector_all(
        ".shipments-table thead th",
        "(els) => els.map(e => e.textContent.trim())",
    )
    assert len(labels) == 15, f"expected 15 thead th, got {len(labels)}"
    assert labels == SPEC_15_COLS, (
        f"§D.8 — column order mismatch\n"
        f"Expected: {SPEC_15_COLS}\nGot:      {labels}"
    )


def test_no_row_selector_checkbox(page):
    assert page.locator("th.col-checkbox").count() == 0
    assert page.locator("td.col-checkbox").count() == 0


def test_no_row_level_copy_or_expand_buttons(page):
    assert page.locator(".copy-trigger").count() == 0
    assert page.locator(".expand-trigger").count() == 0


# ─── §D.9 KPI window toggle ─────────────────────────────────────────

def test_kpi_window_toggle_5_pills(page):
    pills = page.locator(".kpi-window-pill")
    assert pills.count() == 5
    windows = page.eval_on_selector_all(
        ".kpi-window-pill",
        "(els) => els.map(e => e.dataset.window)"
    )
    assert windows == ["today", "week", "month", "quarter", "ytd"]


def test_kpi_window_month_active_by_default(page):
    active = page.locator(".kpi-window-pill.active")
    assert active.count() == 1
    assert active.first.get_attribute("data-window") == "month"


# ─── §D.10 LAN bypass ───────────────────────────────────────────────

def test_auth_js_isLanHost_function_exists():
    """auth.js isn't loaded on shipments.html (which uses LAN bypass by default).
    Verify the function source is in place for pages that DO load auth.js
    (index.html and the portal pages)."""
    auth_js = (OPS / "auth.js").read_text()
    assert "isLanHost" in auth_js
    assert "192.168.1.184" in auth_js
    assert "localhost" in auth_js
    assert "127.0.0.1" in auth_js


def test_shipments_html_has_no_login_overlay_on_lan(page):
    """Spec §D.10 outcome: LAN user sees shipments.html without any login gate."""
    overlay = page.locator(".login-overlay:not(.hidden)")
    assert overlay.count() == 0


# ─── §D.11 Landing route script ─────────────────────────────────────

def test_index_html_has_lan_redirect_script():
    index = (OPS / "index.html").read_text()
    assert "192.168.1.184" in index
    assert "/shipments.html" in index
    # Must be before the portal dashboard content; check it's in <head>
    head_match = re.search(r"<head>(.*?)</head>", index, re.DOTALL)
    assert head_match, "index.html missing <head>"
    head = head_match.group(1)
    assert "location.replace('/shipments.html')" in head, (
        "LAN redirect script must live in <head> so it runs before the portal renders"
    )


V2 UI Completion section gap report:

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
NEW META RULES (apply to entire build, not a single section)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

R-META-1  ANTI-ASSUMPTION RULE
  CC and any code generated by CC must NEVER classify, route, or filter
  any record (customer, invoice, product, P/N, SD) based on assumed
  relationships. Always derive classification from explicit data fields
  on the record itself. Examples:
    - Do NOT infer product family from customer name. Always read line
      items.
    - Do NOT infer customer type from invoice number. Always check the
      Customer Type field on the customer record.
    - Do NOT infer source priority from filename. Always check the
      source_rank metadata.
  When data needed for classification is missing → ROUTE TO HUMAN REVIEW
  QUEUE (§M.5b), do not guess.

R-META-2  HONEST FAILURE
  Every daemon, every parser, every API call: fail loud, never silent.
  If a data point is missing or ambiguous, log it explicitly with
  "CONFIDENCE: LOW, REASON: ..." and surface to Aaron via Tier 2 Telegram.
  Silent fallback to a default value is FORBIDDEN.

R-META-3  NO SHORTCUTS IN HALTS
  When CC HALTs, the HALT message must include: (a) what specifically
  failed, (b) what CC tried, (c) what CC needs from Aaron to resume,
  (d) zero recovery actions taken without explicit Aaron go-ahead per
  V2 §13.

§0.0 (NEW) — PRE-BUILD BACKUP + ROLLBACK PLAN
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Run BEFORE §0 verification. Snapshot current M1 state so V2.2 can be
rolled back cleanly if click-test fails.

  cd ~/norris-ops
  git tag -a pre-v2.2-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S) -m "Pre V2.2 build snapshot"
  git push origin --tags

  cd ~/norris-agent
  git tag -a pre-v2.2-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S) -m "Pre V2.2 build snapshot"
  git push origin --tags

  # Snapshot data directory (registry, ledger, state files)
  mkdir -p ~/norris-agent-backups
  tar czf ~/norris-agent-backups/data-pre-v2.2-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S).tgz \
    -C ~/norris-agent data/

  # Snapshot LaunchAgents in case any get modified
  mkdir -p ~/norris-agent-backups/launchagents-pre-v2.2
  cp ~/Library/LaunchAgents/com.norrisutilities.*.plist \
    ~/norris-agent-backups/launchagents-pre-v2.2/

  # Document rollback procedure to file
  cat > ~/norris-agent-backups/ROLLBACK_V2.2.md << 'EOF'
  # Rollback V2.2 to pre-build state
  
  If V2.2 click-test catastrophically fails and rollback is required:
  
  1. cd ~/norris-ops && git reset --hard pre-v2.2-<TAG>
  2. cd ~/norris-agent && git reset --hard pre-v2.2-<TAG>
  3. Restore data: tar xzf ~/norris-agent-backups/data-pre-v2.2-<TAG>.tgz \
     -C ~/norris-agent
  4. Restore LaunchAgents: cp ~/norris-agent-backups/launchagents-pre-v2.2/*.plist \
     ~/Library/LaunchAgents/
  5. Reload LaunchAgents: launchctl unload then launchctl load each plist
  6. Restart sa-v1-writer: launchctl kickstart -k gui/$UID/com.norrisutilities.sa-v1-writer
  7. Verify preview server :8765 returns 200
  EOF
  echo "Backup and rollback plan staged. Proceed with §0."

§0.5 PATCH — project_knowledge/ population. Discover the latest copy of
each master file on M1 by mtime, symlink into ~/norris-agent/project_knowledge/.
HALT only on genuine absence — not on stale filenames. The same xlsx/csv
files exist in multiple locations on M1; pick newest and use that one.

Run this discovery script as the first step of §0.5 verification:

  mkdir -p ~/norris-agent/project_knowledge
  cd ~/norris-agent/project_knowledge

  # 1) FlexPro Armor pricing master (target: 4.7.26 copy)
  FA=$(find ~ -maxdepth 6 -type f -iname "FlexPro_Armor*Pricing_Master*.xlsx" 2>/dev/null \
    -not -path "*/.Trash/*" -not -path "*/Library/Mobile Documents/*/.*" \
    | xargs -I{} stat -f "%m %N" "{}" 2>/dev/null | sort -rn | head -1 | cut -d' ' -f2-)
  [ -z "$FA" ] && { echo "HALT: FlexPro pricing master missing on M1"; exit 1; }
  ln -sf "$FA" ./FlexPro_Armor_Complete_Pricing_Master.xlsx
  echo "FlexPro master → $FA"

  # 2) QB Contact List (target: 4.17.26 copy)
  QB=$(find ~ -maxdepth 6 -type f \( -iname "QB_Contact_List*.xlsx" -o -iname "*Customer*Contact*List*.xlsx" \) 2>/dev/null \
    -not -path "*/.Trash/*" \
    | xargs -I{} stat -f "%m %N" "{}" 2>/dev/null | sort -rn | head -1 | cut -d' ' -f2-)
  [ -z "$QB" ] && { echo "HALT: QB Contact List missing on M1"; exit 1; }
  ln -sf "$QB" ./QB_Contact_List_with_Addresses.xlsx
  echo "QB Contacts → $QB"

  # 3) FlexPro Direct Price List
  FD=$(find ~ -maxdepth 6 -type f -iname "FlexPro_Armor_Direct_Price_List*.csv" 2>/dev/null \
    | xargs -I{} stat -f "%m %N" "{}" 2>/dev/null | sort -rn | head -1 | cut -d' ' -f2-)
  [ -z "$FD" ] && { echo "HALT: FlexPro Direct Price List missing on M1"; exit 1; }
  ln -sf "$FD" ./FlexPro_Armor_Direct_Price_List.csv
  echo "FlexPro Direct → $FD"

  # 4) Products and Services (xlsx preferred, csv fallback)
  PS=$(find ~ -maxdepth 6 -type f \( -iname "Products*and*Services*Norris*Utilities*.xlsx" -o -iname "ProductServiceList*.csv" \) 2>/dev/null \
    | xargs -I{} stat -f "%m %N" "{}" 2>/dev/null | sort -rn | head -1 | cut -d' ' -f2-)
  [ -z "$PS" ] && { echo "HALT: Products & Services missing on M1"; exit 1; }
  ext="${PS##*.}"
  ln -sf "$PS" "./Products_and_Services.${ext}"
  echo "P&S → $PS"

  # 5) Detailed Sales Report
  DSR=$(find ~ -maxdepth 6 -type f -iname "Detailed_Sales_Report*Product*.csv" 2>/dev/null \
    | xargs -I{} stat -f "%m %N" "{}" 2>/dev/null | sort -rn | head -1 | cut -d' ' -f2-)
  [ -z "$DSR" ] && { echo "HALT: Detailed Sales Report missing on M1"; exit 1; }
  ln -sf "$DSR" ./Detailed_Sales_Report.csv
  echo "Detailed Sales → $DSR"

  # 6) Invoice 1498 PDF (Aaron confirmed location)
  INV="$HOME/Downloads/Invoice_1498_from_Norris_Utilities_LLC.pdf"
  if [ ! -f "$INV" ]; then
    INV=$(find ~ -maxdepth 6 -type f -iname "Invoice*1498*.pdf" 2>/dev/null | head -1)
  fi
  if [ -z "$INV" ] || [ ! -f "$INV" ]; then
    echo "HALT: Invoice 1498 PDF not found"
    exit 1
  fi
  ln -sf "$INV" ./Invoice_1498_LineTec_2026-04-07.pdf
  echo "Invoice 1498 → $INV"

  ls -la ~/norris-agent/project_knowledge/

§0.10 NEW — Pre-flight Gmail credential discovery (run BEFORE proceeding
to §1, after pip install):

  # Discover Legacy's existing Gmail credentials
  GMAIL_CRED_PATHS=(
    "$HOME/norris-agent/credentials/credentials.json"
    "$HOME/norris-agent/.gmail/credentials.json"
    "$HOME/norris-agent/.credentials/credentials.json"
    "$HOME/.norris-agent/credentials.json"
    "$HOME/.credentials/gmail-credentials.json"
    "$HOME/norris-intel/credentials.json"
    "$HOME/Library/Application Support/Norris/credentials.json"
  )
  GMAIL_TOKEN_PATHS=(
    "$HOME/norris-agent/credentials/token.json"
    "$HOME/norris-agent/.gmail/token.json"
    "$HOME/norris-agent/.credentials/token.json"
    "$HOME/.norris-agent/token.json"
    "$HOME/.credentials/gmail-token.json"
    "$HOME/norris-intel/token.json"
    "$HOME/Library/Application Support/Norris/token.json"
  )

  CRED_FOUND=""
  TOKEN_FOUND=""
  for p in "${GMAIL_CRED_PATHS[@]}"; do
    [ -f "$p" ] && { CRED_FOUND="$p"; break; }
  done
  for p in "${GMAIL_TOKEN_PATHS[@]}"; do
    [ -f "$p" ] && { TOKEN_FOUND="$p"; break; }
  done

  # Also check if Legacy's email monitor process has env vars or args
  LEGACY_EMAIL_PROC=$(ps aux | grep -E "email_monitor|gmail" | grep -v grep | head -1)

  # Also check macOS Keychain
  KEYCHAIN_HIT=$(security find-generic-password -s "norris-gmail" 2>/dev/null | head -1)

  if [ -z "$CRED_FOUND" ] || [ -z "$TOKEN_FOUND" ]; then
    echo "HALT §0.10: Gmail credentials not findable in standard paths."
    echo "Searched paths:"
    printf '  %s\n' "${GMAIL_CRED_PATHS[@]}"
    echo ""
    echo "Legacy email_monitor process detected:"
    echo "  $LEGACY_EMAIL_PROC"
    echo ""
    echo "macOS Keychain search for 'norris-gmail':"
    echo "  $KEYCHAIN_HIT"
    echo ""
    echo "Aaron action required (one of):"
    echo "  A) Tell CC where Legacy stores Gmail creds (path)"
    echo "  B) Run a fresh OAuth flow:"
    echo "     1. Visit https://console.cloud.google.com → Create project → Enable Gmail API"
    echo "     2. Create OAuth client ID (Desktop type), download credentials.json"
    echo "     3. Save to ~/norris-agent/credentials/credentials.json"
    echo "     4. Run: cd ~/norris-agent && .venv/bin/python3 bin/gmail_oauth_init.py"
    echo "        (CC creates this script in §M.1 — exists after V2.2 build)"
    echo "     5. Browser opens; click Allow; token.json gets written"
    echo "  Time required: ~5 min for option B"
    exit 1
  fi

  # Verify scopes are sufficient
  python3 -c "
  import json, sys
  with open('$TOKEN_FOUND') as f:
      tok = json.load(f)
  scopes = tok.get('scopes', [])
  required = ['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/gmail.readonly',
              'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/gmail.modify']
  missing = [s for s in required if s not in scopes]
  if missing:
      print(f'HALT §0.10: Gmail token missing required scopes: {missing}')
      print(f'Current scopes: {scopes}')
      print(f'Aaron action: re-run OAuth flow with broader scopes (option B above)')
      sys.exit(1)
  print(f'Gmail credentials OK: {len(scopes)} scopes, all required present')
  "

  # Live test
  python3 -c "
  from google.oauth2.credentials import Credentials
  from googleapiclient.discovery import build
  creds = Credentials.from_authorized_user_file('$TOKEN_FOUND')
  service = build('gmail', 'v1', credentials=creds)
  result = service.users().messages().list(userId='me', q='from:quickbooks@notification.intuit.com', maxResults=1).execute()
  assert result.get('messages'), 'Gmail query returned no results — check creds + permissions'
  print('Gmail live query: PASS')
  "

  # Persist discovered paths for §M.1 to use
  cat > ~/norris-agent/.gmail_paths << EOF
  GMAIL_CREDENTIALS=$CRED_FOUND
  GMAIL_TOKEN=$TOKEN_FOUND
  EOF
  echo "Gmail paths persisted to ~/norris-agent/.gmail_paths"

§0a (NEW) — V1 → V2.2 DATA MIGRATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

V1 customer_registry.json has 82 entries from prior build. V2.2 schema
adds Customer Type enum (Direct/Indirect/Dealer). Migrate:

  python3 ~/norris-agent/bin/migrate_v1_to_v22.py

This script (CC builds it) does:

  1. Load existing customer_registry.json (V1 schema)
  2. For each customer, default Customer Type:
     - "Aerial Hydraulics" → Dealer (Aaron's only current dealer)
     - Customers known to ship via dealer (e.g., Primoris if Aerial
       Hydraulics ships) → Indirect (mark for review)
     - All others → Direct
  3. Add canonical_name field if missing (Company - Person Who Ordered)
  4. Add payment_terms field if missing (default "Due on Receipt")
  5. Add cc_customer flag (default False — Aaron flips per customer)
  6. Add source_rank to all existing data (default SD=85, AARON=80)
  7. Write to customer_registry.json (V2.2 schema)
  8. Write migration report to data/migration_v22.md showing:
     - Customers auto-classified (with reason)
     - Customers marked for human review (no canonical name match)
     - Schema changes applied
  9. Tier 2 Telegram: "✅ V1→V2.2 migration: N customers migrated,
     M flagged for Customer Type review"

Existing shipments_ledger.jsonl entries: leave unchanged (immutable
by §V2 design); new entries use V2.2 schema.

§M (NEW SECTION) — EMAIL AUTOMATION (FULL PRODUCTION WIRING)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

PRINCIPLE: CB never copies, saves, or uploads an invoice. The agent does
it automatically. Aaron stated this verbatim in V1 click-test notes.
Section M is V2.2 scope. Not V3. Not Phase C.

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.1 — Gmail OAuth wire (use existing Legacy credentials, hardened)
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Gmail credential paths discovered by §0.10 are in ~/norris-agent/.gmail_paths.
DO NOT trigger a fresh OAuth flow if creds were found — Aaron has already
authorized.

If §0.10 HALTed because creds not found, Aaron has provided fresh
credentials per §0.10's "Aaron action" path. Build bin/gmail_oauth_init.py
which:

  1. Reads ~/norris-agent/credentials/credentials.json
  2. Runs InstalledAppFlow.from_client_secrets_file with scopes:
     [gmail.readonly, gmail.modify]
  3. Browser opens, Aaron clicks Allow
  4. Token saved to ~/norris-agent/credentials/token.json
  5. Verifies token works (test query)

Build lib/gmail_client.py:

  - Thin wrapper over google-api-python-client
  - Constructor reads ~/norris-agent/.gmail_paths
  - Methods: search(query, max_results), get_message(id),
    get_attachment(message_id, attachment_id, mime_type='application/pdf'),
    mark_processed(message_id, label='SA-Processed')
  - Auto-refresh token if expired (handle Refresh Errors → write log,
    Tier 1 Telegram alert if refresh fails)
  - Rate limit handler: tenacity with exponential backoff on 429
  - Quota tracking: log daily quota consumption to
    ~/norris-agent/data/gmail_quota.jsonl

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.2 — quickbooks@notification.intuit.com watcher (FlexPro Armor invoices)
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Trigger: New email from quickbooks@notification.intuit.com matching
subject pattern: "Invoice [N] from Norris Utilities, LLC" or
"Invoice N from Norris Utilities, LLC" (with or without brackets).

Polling cadence: 5 minutes (separate daemon from Legacy's 3-min monitor).

Pipeline:
  1. Fetch new matching emails since last_seen timestamp
  2. For each email: download PDF attachment via gmail_client.get_attachment
  3. Save PDF to ~/norris-agent/invoices/{NNNN}_{customer_short}_{YYYY-MM-DD}.pdf
  4. Parse PDF with lib/invoice_parser.py — extract:
     - invoice_number, total, line_items (P/N + description + qty + rate),
       subtotal, freight, tax, customer_name (from "Bill To" field),
       invoice_date, due_date
  5. Apply FlexPro Armor product filter (§M.5):
     - REJECT → log to invoice_skipped.jsonl with reason; route to
       human review queue (§M.5b); do NOT auto-update portal
     - ACCEPT → continue
  6. Match to portal SD via lib/invoice_sd_matcher.py:
     - Primary key: customer canonical name fuzzy match (>= 90 score)
     - Secondary: line item P/N overlap >= 50% by P/N count
     - Tertiary: date proximity within 14 days (SD ship date vs invoice date)
     - Edge case: invoice has freight line not on SD → ACCEPT match,
       flag freight as "added in QB" (variance type FREIGHT_ADDED)
     - Edge case: invoice has CC fee line not on SD → ACCEPT match,
       flag as variance type CC_FEE_ADDED
     - Edge case: invoice has additional line item beyond SD → ACCEPT
       match if P/N overlap still >= 50%, flag variance type LINE_ADDED
     - Edge case: invoice missing line item from SD → ACCEPT match if
       P/N overlap still >= 50%, flag variance type LINE_REMOVED
  7. On match:
     - Write actual invoice values to portal SD
     - Mark Invoice Sent = true
     - Set invoice_pdf_path
     - Set invoice_number (clickable link per §M.6)
     - Compute variance: rate_variance, total_variance, type tags
     - Trigger celebration (§M.7 + §S)
     - Log to invoice_ingested.jsonl
     - Tier 2 Telegram (Aaron only — CB has no Telegram per memory):
       "✅ Invoice {NNNN} ingested for {customer_short}, ${total} —
        {N} line items reconciled to SD {SD_ID}, variance: {VARIANCE_TYPE or 'NONE'}"
  8. On no match:
     - Write to portal as orphan invoice (visible in Archived Invoices)
     - Tier 2 Telegram (Aaron): "⚠ Invoice {NNNN} ingested but no SD match
        — review in Archived Invoices"
     - Add to human review queue (§M.5b) with reason NO_SD_MATCH
  9. On match with rate or total variance > 5%:
     - Set row highlight = orange in portal
     - Populate variance tracker UI with deltas
     - Tier 2 Telegram with detailed deltas

LaunchAgent: com.norrisutilities.invoice-watcher
  - StartInterval: 300 (5 min)
  - StandardOutPath / StandardErrorPath:
    ~/norris-agent/logs/invoice-watcher.{out,err}.log
  - KeepAlive: SuccessfulExit=false, NetworkState=true
  - WorkingDirectory: $HOME/norris-agent
  - ProgramArguments: $HOME/norris-agent/.venv/bin/python3,
    $HOME/norris-agent/bin/invoice_watcher.py

State file: ~/norris-agent/data/invoice_watcher_state.json
  - last_processed_message_id
  - last_processed_timestamp
  - processed_message_ids (rolling 30-day set, dedup guard)
  - quota_consumed_today
  - last_heartbeat

§M.2.1 — 30-DAY HISTORICAL BACKFILL (first run only)

On first run after V2.2 ship, watcher runs ONE-TIME backfill:
  - Query Gmail: from:quickbooks@notification.intuit.com subject:Invoice
    after:30days_ago
  - Process every matching email through the same pipeline (steps 2-9)
  - Tier 1 Telegram: "✅ V2.2 backfill complete: N FlexPro invoices
    ingested, M skipped (non-FlexPro), K orphans for review"
  - After backfill, write backfill_complete=true to state file
  - Subsequent runs only process new emails since last_processed_timestamp

§M.2.2 — DAILY RECONCILIATION AGAINST QB

LaunchAgent: com.norrisutilities.qb-reconcile
  - Runs daily at 4:00 AM CT
  - Queries Intuit QuickBooks MCP (already connected per available tools)
    to get all invoices created/modified in last 24 hours
  - Compares against portal: any invoice CB voided or edited that
    didn't trigger a Gmail notification?
  - For voids: update portal SD to set invoice_voided=true,
    invoice_sent=false, append to ledger, Tier 2 Telegram
  - For edits: detect total/line changes, update portal, Tier 2 Telegram
  - For invoices in QB but not in portal: log to recon_gap.jsonl,
    Tier 2 Telegram
  - Reconciliation report written to ~/norris-agent/data/qb_recon_{DATE}.md

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.3 — UPS delivery confirmation email watcher
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Trigger: New email from pkginfo@ups.com / mcinfo@ups.com /
auto-notify@ups.com / quantumview@ups.com matching subject containing
"delivered" or "Delivery Notification".

Pipeline:
  1. Parse tracking number from email body (UPS format: 1Z + 16 chars)
  2. Look up tracking in portal shipments
  3. If found → status = Delivered, set delivered_date from email body
     (parse with python-dateutil for flexibility), trigger small
     celebration (§S delivered.wav), Tier 3 Telegram (batched daily)
  4. Log to delivery_confirmed.jsonl
  5. Edge case: tracking not in portal → log to delivery_unmatched.jsonl,
     do NOT alert (some UPS emails are for non-NU shipments)

LaunchAgent: com.norrisutilities.delivery-watcher
  - Same cadence and structure as invoice-watcher
  - Separate state file: data/delivery_watcher_state.json

Honest scope note: UPS does not email delivery confirmation for every
service level. Ground service typically does; Surepost / Mail Innovations
may not. Estimate ~70-85% delivery coverage via email; UPS API polling
(V3 deferred) closes the remaining gap. For V2.2 production: this is
sufficient; CB or Aaron can manually mark Delivered for the 15-30%
gap via the status pill (already in V2 §3).

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.4 — PDF download + filename normalization
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  - Download via gmail_client.get_attachment(message_id, attachment_id)
  - Validate magic bytes (%PDF-)
  - Compute normalized filename:
    {invoice_number}_{customer_short}_{YYYY-MM-DD}.pdf
    where customer_short = recipient email domain stripped (e.g.,
    "ltspower" from BVanderhoeven@ltspower.com)
  - Save to ~/norris-agent/invoices/
  - chmod 644
  - Symlink ~/norris-ops/internal/invoices/{NNNN}.pdf → above path
    (so portal serves on same domain, auth-gated)
  - On filename collision (rare): append _v2, _v3, etc., Tier 2 Telegram

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.5 — FlexPro Armor product filter (the M5 misclassification fix)
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Build lib/product_family.py with:

  def is_flexpro_armor(line_items: list[dict]) -> tuple[bool, str]:
      """
      Returns (accepted, reason).
      
      ACCEPT (True) if at least 25% of line items by count are FlexPro:
        - P/N starts with NU-BC- (any bucket cover variant including
          NU-BC-2828, NU-BC-2834, NU-BC-2851, NU-BC-BY2828, NU-BC-D-Shape,
          NU-BC-2834-F, NU-BC-2851-F, NU-BC-2834-C, NU-BC-2851-C, etc.)
        - P/N starts with NU-TB- (tool board)
        - P/N starts with NU-DT- (dirt tarp)
        - Description contains case-insensitive: "flexpro", "bucket cover",
          "tool board", "dirt tarp", "bucket cvr"
      
      REJECT (False) if ZERO FlexPro line items, or if FlexPro count <
      25% of total non-shipping/non-CC-fee line items:
        Reason taxonomy:
          NO_FLEXPRO_LINES
          MOSTLY_ROPE (Samson P/N patterns: 80*, 86*, 87*, 96*; or
            description containing "Tenex", "Stable Braid", "AmSteel",
            "Nylite", "Spool")
          MOSTLY_RENTAL (description containing "rental", "lease",
            "monthly rate")
          MOSTLY_TRUCK (P/N starts with SBA, or BSS TR2/TR3, or 
            description containing "bucket truck", "aerial lift")
          UNKNOWN_PRODUCT_FAMILY (no recognized pattern)
      """

Test fixtures (must all pass — written into the test suite):
  - Invoice_1498 (FlexPro for LineTec, $354.75) → (True, "FLEXPRO")
  - Invoice_1439 (Samson rope for MS Power) → (False, "MOSTLY_ROPE")
  - Synthetic mixed (3 BC + 1 small rope) → (True, "FLEXPRO_MAJORITY")
  - Synthetic mostly-rope (5 ropes + 1 BC) → (False, "MOSTLY_ROPE")

This filter MUST be called by §M.2 step 5. No bypass. No "trust the
subject line." No customer-name shortcuts. Line items are the only
source of truth.

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.5b — HUMAN REVIEW QUEUE (NEW)
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

New portal page: /internal/review_queue.html (auth: norris2026 + legacy2026)

Surfaces invoices and SDs that need human attention because automation
can't make a confident call. Categories:

  - REJECTED_FILTER: §M.5 said reject; Aaron can review and "Force Ingest"
    (override into FlexPro pipeline) if filter was wrong
  - NO_SD_MATCH: invoice ingested but no SD found; orphan invoice waiting
    for human to attach to correct SD or mark as standalone
  - HIGH_VARIANCE: variance > 5% on rate/total; needs human verification
  - MISSING_CUSTOMER_TYPE: V2.2 migration flagged a customer with
    ambiguous Customer Type (Direct/Indirect/Dealer)
  - PARSE_FAIL: PDF parse failed entirely; needs manual entry

UI:
  - Card per item with: source data, suggested action, "Approve",
    "Reject", "Edit", "Skip" buttons
  - Aaron's preferences default to surfacing all queue items in morning
    brief (Tier 2 batch); CB sees only queue items where Aaron has
    approved her to action

LaunchAgent: com.norrisutilities.review-queue-monitor
  - Daily 4:00 AM CT (with morning brief)
  - If queue depth > 0: Tier 2 Telegram "⚠ Review queue: N items
    awaiting Aaron decision"

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.6 — Inv. # link in portal → opens auto-saved PDF
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Inv. # column becomes hyperlink when invoice_pdf_path is populated:

  <a href="/internal/invoices/{NNNN}.pdf" target="_blank"
     class="inv-link" title="Open Invoice {NNNN} PDF">
    {NNNN}
  </a>

If invoice_pdf_path not populated → render as plain text, grey color.

Auth: /internal/invoices/ inherits legacy2026 + norris2026 access (CB
CAN open invoice PDFs).

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.7 — Auto-celebrate on new invoice ingest
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Hook into existing celebration_engine.py (V1, extended in V2):

  - Tier: invoice_ingested (NEW between mark_shipped and full_pay)
  - Trigger: §M.2 step 7 success
  - Visual: confetti + invoice number flyup + checkmark animation on
    SD row
  - Sound: chime.wav (§S)
  - Telegram: same Tier 2 ping as §M.2 (do not double-fire)
  - Persist: celebration_log entry — refresh shows celebration ribbon
    for 24 hours after ingest

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.8 — Daemon health + observability + rate limit handling
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  - Heartbeat: each watcher writes ~/norris-agent/data/heartbeat_{name}.json
    every cycle
  - If heartbeat older than 15 min → Tier 1 Telegram
  - Failure threshold: 3 consecutive cycle failures → LaunchAgent KeepAlive
    restarts; if 5 restarts in 15 min → Tier 1 Telegram, daemon enters
    cooldown (60 min) to avoid loops
  - Gmail rate limits: tenacity exponential backoff, max 5 retries
    (1s, 2s, 4s, 8s, 16s); on persistent 429 → cooldown 1 hour, Tier 2
  - Daily Gmail quota tracking: log to gmail_quota.jsonl; Aaron alert
    if >75% of daily quota consumed
  - Log retention: rotate logs >10MB to ~/norris-agent/logs/archive/
    via separate LaunchAgent com.norrisutilities.log-rotate (daily 3AM CT)
  - Add daemon status to /internal/health.html — show last heartbeat,
    last success, last error per watcher

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.9 — Time zone standardization
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

All timestamps stored in UTC ISO-8601 format. All UI display in
America/Chicago (CT) with explicit TZ suffix on relative times.
All daemon schedules in CT (4:00 AM CT, etc.) — LaunchAgent plists
use local time which is CT on M1.

  - Use pytz: TZ_CT = pytz.timezone('America/Chicago')
  - Email date headers (often UTC or sender TZ) parsed by
    email.utils.parsedate_to_datetime, then converted to UTC for
    storage, then to CT for display
  - Invoice dates from PDF (often local TZ-naive) treated as CT,
    converted to UTC for storage

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.10 — Aaron manual override on misclassified invoices
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

In review_queue.html, REJECTED_FILTER items have a "Force Ingest" button.
Clicking it:
  1. Marks the invoice as aaron_force_ingest=true in invoice metadata
  2. Re-runs §M.2 from step 6 (skipping §M.5 filter)
  3. Logs override to ~/norris-agent/data/filter_overrides.jsonl (audit
     trail; if pattern emerges Aaron can adjust §M.5 thresholds)
  4. Tier 2 Telegram: "🔧 Aaron overrode §M.5 reject for invoice {NNNN}
      — investigating filter quality"

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
§M.11 — Telegram notification routing (clarification)
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Tier 1 (immediate, blocking — Aaron only @NorrisLegacyBot):
  - HALTs from any watcher
  - Daemon failure cooldowns
  - Auth/credential issues
  - Henkels R8 historical correction notice
  - V2.2 build complete

Tier 2 (within 15 min — Aaron only):
  - Invoice ingested (success)
  - Variance flagged (high)
  - Review queue depth alert
  - QB recon discrepancy
  - Aaron filter override

Tier 3 (batched daily 6 PM CT — Aaron only):
  - UPS delivery confirmations
  - Invoice ingest success summaries
  - Quota usage report

CB has no Telegram (per memory: "CB Telegram Bot pending — separate bot,
business-only, no personal info"). CB's notification surface is the
portal itself + email if Aaron forwards. V2.2 does NOT send anything
to CB directly. When CB Telegram Bot ships in a future session, route
Tier 2 invoice celebrations to her separately.

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
§S (NEW SECTION) — CELEBRATION SOUNDS (graceful degradation)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  - assets/sounds/ directory:
      chime.wav         (invoice_ingested, 0.4s, mid-vol)
      cha-ching.wav     (full_pay, 0.8s, louder)
      delivered.wav     (UPS delivery, 0.3s, soft)
      mark-shipped.wav  (status → Shipped, 0.2s, neutral)
      mega.wav          (mega celebration, 1.2s, full-vol)

  - Sound source fallback chain (CC tries in order):
      1. Download from freesound.org (royalty-free; CC vets license =
         CC0 or CC-BY-attribution and embeds attribution in
         assets/sounds/ATTRIBUTION.md)
      2. If download blocked / network failure: generate via Web Audio
         API tone synthesis (oscillator + envelope, simple beep
         variants per sound)
      3. If both fail: silent no-op (visual celebration still fires)

  - assets/js/sound-engine.js:
      - On first user click anywhere in portal → unlock AudioContext
        (Chrome autoplay policy compliance), set audioUnlocked=true
        in sessionStorage
      - play(soundName) function: if !audioUnlocked → silent no-op;
        else play at user volume preference (default 60%)
      - Errors caught, logged to console, never thrown

  - User preferences page /internal/preferences.html (NEW or extend
    existing):
      - Celebration Sounds toggle (default ON for Aaron, OFF for CB)
      - Volume slider (0-100%, default 60%)
      - Per-sound mute (e.g., user might mute mark-shipped but keep
        invoice_ingested)

  - Tier 4 (silent build verification): pytest checks that
    sound-engine.play() never throws under any test condition

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
§R (NEW SECTION) — LIGHTWEIGHT CUSTOMER REPLY SURFACE
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

DECISION POINT FOR AARON: Customer reply NLP / auto-response is
genuinely a separate scope (NLP model, intent detection, response
generation, risk of bad auto-replies damaging customer relationships).
Three options:

  (a) Full NLP + auto-respond — adds ~6-10 hr build, RISK: bad
      auto-reply sent without Aaron review. Not recommended without
      a separate design session on tone matching and risk controls.

  (b) RECOMMENDED — Lightweight surface (build in V2.2): parse
      incoming customer emails on QB invoice notification threads,
      extract intent signal (question / acknowledgment / payment /
      complaint / dispute) using simple rule-based classifier (no LLM
      call), surface to Aaron via Telegram and review_queue.html
      for human action. NO auto-response sent.

  (c) Defer entirely to V3 (separate session)

V2.2 IMPLEMENTS (b): lib/customer_reply_classifier.py + integration
into §M.2 watcher.

  - When QB notification thread receives a reply (sender != quickbooks@
    and != Norris Utilities domain), capture in customer_replies.jsonl
  - Classifier rules (regex-based, no LLM):
      ACK: "thanks", "got it", "received"
      PAYMENT: "paid", "payment", "ach", "check sent"
      QUESTION: "?", "what is", "could you", "can you", "when"
      DISPUTE: "wrong", "incorrect", "shouldn't", "not what we ordered"
      COMPLAINT: "frustrated", "disappointed", "unacceptable"
      OTHER: anything else
  - Tier 2 Telegram on each reply: "💬 Customer reply ({intent}) on
     Invoice {NNNN} from {sender}: '{snippet}'"
  - Add to review_queue.html under category CUSTOMER_REPLY
  - Aaron acts manually; V2.2 makes ZERO auto-responses

3.1  STATUS PILL MARKUP
     Column 2 in the table (per E.2). Each row cell renders:
       <button class="status-pill status-{status}" data-shipment-id="{id}"
               aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0">
         <span class="status-dot"></span>
         <span class="status-label">{STATUS_UPPER}</span>
         <svg class="caret" ...>▼</svg>
       </button>

3.2  STATUS VALUES (7 locked)
     • pending    — slate gray (#6B7280)
     • processing — amber (#F59E0B)
     • shipped    — blue (#0066EE)
     • invoiced   — green (#10B981)
     • cc         — teal (#06D0FF)       (CC charged / held for charge)
     • blocked    — red (#DC2626)
     • REVIEW     — orange pulsing (#FB923C, subtle pulse 2s)

3.3  DROPDOWN BEHAVIOR
     Click or Enter/Space on pill:
       - Opens <ul role="listbox"> below pill
       - 7 options, each <li role="option"> with same color dot + label
       - Keyboard: Arrow up/down navigates, Enter selects, Esc closes
       - Click outside = close
       - Only one open at a time
     On selection:
       - POST (via fetch) to update endpoint (or direct JSON write if
         daemonless V1 — see 3.4)
       - On success: pill updates, celebration fires, audit appends,
         ledger event written
       - On failure: pill reverts, toast "Status update failed" + retry

3.4  V1 UPDATE ENDPOINT (no Phase C daemons yet)
     Since Phase C daemons aren't live, Phase B uses a minimal endpoint:
       POST /api/shipments/<id>/status (bound to simple Python handler)
     OR client-side direct write:
       - fetch shipments.json
       - apply change
       - PUT back via simple file-write endpoint
     
     RECOMMENDED: Stand up a tiny FastAPI or Python http.server handler
     on port 8766 that:
       - Reads/writes ~/norris-agent/data/shipments.json (atomic write
         via tempfile + rename)
       - Appends to ~/norris-agent/data/shipments_ledger.jsonl
       - Returns updated shipment record
     
     LaunchAgent (NEW):
       ~/Library/LaunchAgents/com.norrisutilities.sa-v1-writer.plist
       - Runs: python3 ~/norris-agent/bin/sa_v1_writer.py
       - Port: 8766
       - Label: com.norrisutilities.sa-v1-writer
       - RunAtLoad: true
       - KeepAlive: true
       - StandardErrorPath: /tmp/sa-v1-writer.err
       - StandardOutPath:   /tmp/sa-v1-writer.out

3.5  AUDIT LOG SCHEMA (lib/audit_log.py + data/audit_log.jsonl)
     Every status change writes an audit entry:
     {
       "id": "audit_<uuid4>",
       "shipment_id": "S-2026-023",
       "actor": "aaron" | "cb" | "sa_auto" | "legacy_auto",
       "iso_ts": "2026-04-23T17:23:45-05:00",
       "display_ts": "Apr 23 5:23 PM CT",
       "event": "status_change",
       "from": "shipped",
       "to": "invoiced",
       "source": "aaron_click" | "cb_click" | "qb_webhook" |
                 "gmail_parse" | "ups_poll" | "sa_derived",
       "notes": "" (optional freeform)
     }
     Store: ~/norris-agent/data/audit_log.jsonl (append-only)
     Also kept per-shipment inside shipments.json under shipment.audit_trail[]
     (max last 20 entries in-row; full history via separate file).

3.6  SHIPMENTS LEDGER (lib/ledger.py + data/shipments_ledger.jsonl)
     Append-only, NEVER pruned. Captures every event permanently from now on.
     Enables Phase-D+ KPI dashboards (Q17) that read full historical replay.
     
     Event schema:
     {
       "ledger_id": "led_<uuid4>",
       "ts": "2026-04-23T17:23:45-05:00",
       "shipment_id": "S-2026-023",
       "event_type": "status_change" | "notes_edit" | "invoice_sent" |
                     "alias_added" | "archive" | "unarchive" |
                     "celebration_fired" | "mega_fired",
       "actor": "...",
       "data": { ... event-specific payload ... },
       "dedup_key": sha256(customer + invoice# + event_type + date_to_minute)
                    (used by Phase C for cross-validator dedup)
     }

3.7  STANDARD CELEBRATION MAPPING
     from_state → to_state → celebration id:
       pending    → processing = "sparkle"          (1.5s)
       processing → shipped    = "confetti-burst"   (3s)
       shipped    → invoiced   = "phoenix-rise"     (5s, plays chime)
       invoiced   → cc         = "ka-ching"         (2s, green check pulse)
       any        → blocked    = "red-flash"        (0.5s, no sound)
       any        → REVIEW     = "amber-pulse"      (1s, no sound)
       status_change reversed  = none (no reverse celebration)
     Implementation: celebration-engine.js exposes
       CelebrationEngine.fire(id, anchorEl)
     Where anchorEl is the status pill or row for positioning.

3.8  MEGA-CELEBRATIONS (5 triggers, rare, milestone)
     Fired by status_engine.py after every status change, checking
     post-change state of the whole queue. Priority order (at most one
     per event):

     Trigger M1 — QUEUE CLEARED
       Condition: count(shipments where status != invoiced AND
                         invoice_sent != true) drops from >0 to 0
       Effect (8–10 seconds):
         - Full-screen overlay fades in (cyan/blue gradient @ 50% opacity)
         - Large phoenix graphic bursts from center, scales 0 → 1.5 → 1
         - Confetti rains from top for 6 seconds (blue/cyan/white)
         - Text banner: "QUEUE CLEARED!" (Lato Black 900, 5rem)
         - Sub-banner: "Would Wayne be proud of this? Hell yes."
           (Playfair italic 1.5rem, appears 2s in, fades 2s out)
         - Triumphant 3-tone chime (if browser audio unlocked)
         - Click-anywhere dismisses early
         - Auto-dismiss at 10s

     Trigger M2 — CENTURY MARK
       Condition: count(shipments with status=invoiced in current month)
                  crosses from 99 to 100
       Effect (5s):
         - Gold confetti cascade from top
         - Banner: "100th invoice of the month! 💯"
         - Sub-banner: "That's a whole lot of shipping done right."

     Trigger M3 — SHIP GONNA SAIL SMOOTH
       Condition: Unbilled Revenue tile transitions from >$0 to $0
       Effect (4s):
         - Boat emoji 🚢 floats across screen left to right
         - Banner: "All billed. Ship gonna sail smooth."
         - Gentle wave animation at bottom

     Trigger M4 — FIRST SHIPMENT OF THE DAY
       Condition: First status change to "shipped" after 4 AM CT
       Effect (2s):
         - Target emoji 🎯 appears, subtle zoom 0.8 → 1.1 → 1
         - Banner: "First shipment fired 🎯"
         - Subtle cyan shimmer across hero

     Trigger M5 — TEN CLEAN STREAK
       Condition: 10 consecutive status=invoiced events with NO intervening
                  REVIEW status (tracked in ledger)
       Effect (3s):
         - Fire emojis 🔥 burst from bottom
         - Banner: "On a roll! 10 clean 🔥"
         - Counter flashes "10" three times

     Rate limits:
       - Same mega won't fire twice in the same browser session
       - Mega overrides standard celebration (standard is suppressed
         when mega fires)
       - Never fires on reverse/undo events
       - Never fires for negative events (blocked, REVIEW)

     Implementation file: ~/norris-ops/assets/js/mega-celebrations.js
     Audio files (optional; silent fallback if missing):
       ~/norris-ops/assets/audio/chime.mp3 (short, 2s, royalty-free)
       ~/norris-ops/assets/audio/victory.mp3 (longer, 3s, for M1)

3.9  HOVER TOOLTIP ON STATUS PILL
     Show last audit entry:
       "Changed from shipped → invoiced by Aaron on Apr 23 5:23 PM CT"
     If no history yet: "No status history"
     Tooltip element: <div class="status-tooltip"> anchored below pill,
     150ms fade-in on 500ms hover delay.
     "View Full History" link inside tooltip → opens modal with full
     audit trail for that shipment (see Section 4.6).

     test_status_pill_interactive.py:
       - pill renders with correct color per status
       - click opens dropdown
       - keyboard nav (Tab, Arrow, Enter, Esc)
       - select fires update + audit + ledger + celebration event

       - M2 fires on 99->100 invoiced-this-month

checkbox (column 15) tick archives row with confetti + toast + slide-out.

5.1  NOTES CELL — READ MODE
     <td class="notes-cell" data-shipment-id="{id}" tabindex="0"
         aria-label="Notes for shipment {id}">
       <span class="notes-text">{notes | truncate(80)}</span>
       {if len(notes) > 80:}
       <span class="notes-more">(click to read)</span>
       {end if}
     </td>
     - Wrap text up to 80 chars in the cell
     - Click or Enter/Space → enter edit mode
     - Hover shows pencil icon ✎ faintly

5.2  NOTES CELL — EDIT MODE
     On activate:
       - Replace span with <textarea class="notes-editor" rows="3"
         maxlength="2000">{notes}</textarea>
       - Auto-focus textarea, cursor at end
       - Show character counter: {len}/2000
       - Show action bar: [Save (Cmd+Enter)] [Cancel (Esc)]
     On Save (blur OR Cmd+Enter OR click Save):
       - POST to sa-v1-writer /api/shipments/{id}/notes with {notes: new_value}
       - On success: render new notes, append audit + ledger:
           {event: "notes_edit", from: old, to: new, actor: "aaron" | "cb"}
         Toast: "Notes saved" (2s, cyan)
       - On failure: keep edit mode open, toast: "Save failed — retry"
     On Cancel (Esc or click Cancel):
       - Revert to original, no write, no audit
     Clicking outside cell = Save (same as blur)

5.3  NOTES CELL — AUTO-SAVE DEBOUNCE
     While editing, debounce writes:
       - After 3s of no typing → silent auto-save (no toast)
       - Still writes audit on change committed
       - Prevents data loss on tab close mid-edit

5.4  INVOICE SENT CHECKBOX — COLUMN 15
     <td class="invoice-sent-cell">
       <label class="invoice-sent">
         <input type="checkbox" class="invoice-sent-box"
                data-shipment-id="{id}" {checked if invoice_sent}>
         <span class="checkmark"></span>
       </label>
     </td>

5.5  ON TICK
     1. Optimistic UI: checkbox ticks, row fades slightly
     2. POST /api/shipments/{id}/invoice-sent {sent: true}
     3. sa_v1_writer.py:
        - Sets invoice_sent = true
        - If status != "invoiced", sets status = "invoiced" (audit event)
        - Appends audit: event="invoice_sent", actor, ts
        - Appends ledger: event_type="invoice_sent"
        - Returns updated shipment
     4. On success (frontend):
        - Confetti burst (500ms) at the checkbox position
        - Toast: "Invoice sent — archived" (3s, green)
        - Row slide-out animation (500ms, translateX(100%) + opacity 0 → 0)
        - After 500ms: remove <tr> from DOM
        - Update PULSE tiles (Open count -1, etc.)
        - If this was the LAST open SD → fires mega M1 (queue cleared)
        - If this was the 100th invoiced in the month → fires mega M2
        - If unbilled revenue now $0 (post-change) → fires mega M3
        - Check M5 (10 clean streak) — fires if applicable
     5. On failure: revert checkbox, toast "Archive failed — retry"

5.6  ON UNTICK (reverse)
     - Confirm dialog: "Un-archive this shipment? Status will revert to
       previous state. This creates an audit entry."
     - On confirm:
        - POST /api/shipments/{id}/invoice-sent {sent: false}
        - sa_v1_writer.py:
          - invoice_sent = false
          - status = previous_status (from last audit entry before
            invoice_sent tick)
          - audit: event="invoice_sent_reverse"
          - ledger: event_type="unarchive"
        - Frontend: row re-renders in main table (position: alphabetical
          by customer), NO celebration, no confetti
        - Toast: "Un-archived" (2s, neutral)

5.7  ATOMIC WRITE (shipments_writer.py)
     def write_shipment(shipment_id, updates: dict) -> dict:
       """Atomic update to shipments.json. tempfile + rename. Returns
       updated full record."""
       path = Path.home() / "norris-agent/data/shipments.json"
       with FileLock(str(path) + ".lock"):
           data = json.loads(path.read_text())
           idx = next(i for i, s in enumerate(data["shipments"])
                      if s["id"] == shipment_id)
           data["shipments"][idx].update(updates)
           # Write to temp, fsync, rename
           tmp = path.with_suffix(".tmp")
           tmp.write_text(json.dumps(data, indent=2))
           os.fsync(...)
           tmp.rename(path)
           return data["shipments"][idx]

6.1  FUZZY MATCH IMPLEMENTATION (fuzzy_match.py)
     from rapidfuzz import fuzz, process

     def score_candidate(raw: str, entry: dict) -> int:
         """Return 0–100 confidence that raw matches this registry entry."""
         base = 0

         # Exact match on canonical_name
         if raw.strip().lower() == entry["canonical_name"].strip().lower():
             return 100

         # company_root token-set match
         company_score = fuzz.token_set_ratio(
             raw, entry["company_root"]
         )  # 0-100
         base = company_score * 0.6  # max 60 from company

         # Alias exact match +20
         if any(raw.strip().lower() == a.strip().lower()
                for a in entry.get("aliases", [])):
             base += 20

         # POC match (if raw contains a person-like substring) +30
         poc = entry.get("poc", "")
         if poc and fuzz.partial_ratio(poc, raw) > 85:
             base += 30

         # Branch/location match +10
         branch = entry.get("branch", "")
         if branch and fuzz.partial_ratio(branch, raw) > 85:
             base += 10

         return min(int(base), 100)

     def match_customer(raw: str, registry: list) -> dict:
         """Return {best, candidates, tier, action}."""
         scored = sorted(
             [(score_candidate(raw, e), e) for e in registry],
             key=lambda x: -x[0]
         )
         best_score, best_entry = scored[0] if scored else (0, None)
         candidates = [
             {"entry_id": e["id"], "canonical_name": e["canonical_name"],
              "score": s}
             for s, e in scored[:3] if s > 40
         ]
         if best_score >= 95:
             tier = "auto_apply"
             action = "apply"
         elif best_score >= 80:
             tier = "flag"
             action = "apply_with_flag"
         else:
             tier = "review"
             action = "mark_review"
         return {
             "best": best_entry,
             "best_score": best_score,
             "candidates": candidates,
             "tier": tier,
             "action": action,
         }

6.2  add_alias() FUNCTION (registry_loader.py)
     def add_alias(entry_id: str, new_alias: str, confidence: int,
                   source: str = "sa_auto") -> dict:
         """Append alias to entry. Atomic. Ledger event written."""
         path = Path.home() / "norris-agent/data/customer_registry.json"
         with FileLock(str(path) + ".lock"):
             registry = json.loads(path.read_text())
             entry = next(e for e in registry if e["id"] == entry_id)
             if new_alias in entry.get("aliases", []):
                 return {"success": False, "reason": "duplicate",
                         "entry_id": entry_id, "alias": new_alias}
             entry.setdefault("aliases", []).append(new_alias)
             tmp = path.with_suffix(".tmp")
             tmp.write_text(json.dumps(registry, indent=2))
             os.fsync(...)
             tmp.rename(path)
         # Ledger
         ledger.append({
             "ledger_id": f"led_{uuid.uuid4().hex}",
             "ts": datetime.now(ZoneInfo("America/Chicago")).isoformat(),
             "shipment_id": None,
             "event_type": "alias_added",
             "actor": source,
             "data": {
                 "entry_id": entry_id,
                 "alias": new_alias,
                 "confidence": confidence,
             },
         })
         return {"success": True, "entry_id": entry_id,
                 "alias": new_alias, "confidence": confidence}

6.4  CANONICAL ENFORCEMENT (canonical_enforce.py)
     CANONICAL_RE = re.compile(r"^[A-Za-z0-9&\-\.\s]+ - [A-Za-z\s\.]+$")
     
     def is_canonical(name: str) -> bool:
         return bool(CANONICAL_RE.match(name))
     
     def scan_registry() -> list:
         """Return list of entries whose canonical_name violates format."""
         registry = load_registry()
         violations = []
         for e in registry:
             if not is_canonical(e["canonical_name"]):
                 violations.append({
                     "entry_id": e["id"],
                     "canonical_name": e["canonical_name"],
                     "company_root": e.get("company_root", ""),
                     "poc": e.get("poc", ""),
                     "reason": (
                         "missing person" if " - " not in e["canonical_name"]
                         else "format mismatch"
                     ),
                 })
         return violations

     Run at build time in registry_remediation.py → write violations to
     ~/norris-agent/data/customer_registry_review.csv with a column
     "canonical_violation=true". Aaron resolves during later review pass.

6.5  REGISTRY REMEDIATION SCAN (registry_remediation.py)
     Runs once. Iterates all 82 registry entries:
       1. If canonical violation → try to propose fix
          a. If entry has poc → canonical = f"{company_root} - {poc}"
          b. If no poc → scan SD HTML files for orderer name associated
             with this company_root → propose candidates
          c. If no signal → flag for Aaron as "needs_orderer"
       2. Write proposal to customer_registry_review.csv with columns:
          entry_id, current_canonical, proposed_canonical, reason,
          source_evidence, action_needed
       3. Do NOT auto-apply without Aaron's explicit approval
     
     Output: appends to existing customer_registry_review.csv
     (don't overwrite — append a new section with a timestamp header).

  INPUTS (read-only):

    (or newer; find latest)
